First of all, the hotel is located in a remote area, and it is not convenient to go anywhere. You can take the hotel shuttle bus. But the shuttle bus is not convenient, and it is infuriating to take the bus several times. You have to wait for 20 minutes for a 10-minute ride, and it is said to be a traffic jam. I looked at the navigation and there was no traffic jam at all. He just wanted to pick up more guests at one time and let you wait at the station in vain. There was not a single truth. The most infuriating thing was that on the second night, it was raining heavily. We walked to the designated pick-up point with difficulty. After waiting for more than 20 minutes, he called us to go to another station to take the bus, saying that the road was closed. But we saw cars coming and going at the place where we were waiting for the bus. He only thought about how to make it convenient for himself, and didn't care about the situation of the guests at all. In addition, the hotel's car can obviously go directly to the Meilu Villa scenic spot. When I asked the driver if he could go directly to the scenic spot, the driver deliberately didn't answer, and asked you to get off at one more station and then queue up to go back. I really can't understand how people with this mentality can provide good service?
There is no scenery from the hotel room.
The triple room only comes with two pairs of slippers. I took a hot shower, but the water became dirtier and dirtier halfway through (see the picture below) and there was no hot water in the end. It's a rip-off.
In short, it's not worth it. The attitude of the service staff is wrong. I won't stay here again.
